queueCond.wait(lock, [&]() {\n                    return processingStop.load() || !messageQueue.empty();\n                });\n                if (processingStop.load() && messageQueue.empty()) {\n                    return;\n                }\n                msg = std::move(messageQueue.front());\n                messageQueue.pop_front();\n            }\n\n            // ------------------------------------------------------------\n            //  Per-message processing\n            // ------------------------------------------------------------\n            try {\n                if (msg.get_key()) {\n                    spdlog::trace(\"Consumed key: {}\", msg.get_key());\n                }\n\n                nlohmann::json payload = nlohmann::json::parse(msg.get_payload());\n                const auto&    eventType = payload.at(\"eventType\").get_ref<const std::string&>();\n                dispatcher_->dispatch(eventType, payload);\n\n                // Commit offset manually (synchronously for simplicity)\n                if (!config_.enableAutoCommit) {\n                    consumer_.commit(msg);\n                }\n            }\n            catch (const nlohmann::json::parse_error& ex) {\n                log_->error(\"JSON parse error at offset {}: {}\", msg.get_offset(), ex.what());\n            }\n            catch (const nlohmann::json::out_of_range& ex) {\n                log_->error(\"Missing required JSON fields: {}\", ex.what());\n            }\n            catch (const std::exception& ex) {\n                log_->error(\"Unhandled exception while processing message: {}\", ex.what());\n            }\n        }\n    };\n\n    // Spawn processing threads\n    for (size_t i = 0; i < config_.maxProcessingThreads; ++i) {\n        processingThreads.emplace_back(workerFn);\n    }\n\n    // Main polling loop\n    while (running_.load()) {\n        try {\n            auto msg = consumer_.poll(config_.pollTimeout);\n\n            if (!msg) {\n                continue; // timeout\n            }\n\n            if (msg.get_error()) {\n                // End-of-partition or error\n                if (!msg.is_eof()) {\n                    log_->error(\"Kafka error: {}\", msg.get_error());\n                }\n                continue;\n            }\n\n            // Enqueue message\n            {\n                std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(queueMutex);\n                messageQueue.emplace_back(std::move(msg));\n            }\n            queueCond.notify_one();\n        }\n        catch (const cppkafka::HandleException& ex) {\n            log_->error(\"Kafka exception: {}\", ex.what());\n        }\n        catch (const std::exception& ex) {\n            log_->error(\"Unexpected exception: {}\", ex.what());\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Signal processing threads to finish\n    {\n        std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(queueMutex);\n        processingStop.store(true);\n    }\n    queueCond.notify_all();\n\n    // Join processing threads\n    for (auto& t : processingThreads) {\n        if (t.joinable()) {\n            t.join();\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n//--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n//  Example stub dispatcher (to be implemented in domain layer)\n//--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n#if 0   // Example usage (disabled by default)\n\nclass DemoDispatcher : public }\n\n    std::unique_ptr<IScanStrategy> makeStrategy(ScanIntensity in)\n    {\n        switch (in)\n        {\n        case ScanIntensity::kLight: return std::make_unique<LightScanStrategy>(log_);\n Scanner Engine - THE BOTTLENECK (Single FIFO Queue)\n\n```cpp\n// File: /app/project/src/services/scanner_svc/scanner_engine.cpp\n// Lines: 198-241\n\ntemplate <typename T>\nclass BlockingQueue\n{\npublic:\n    explicit BlockingQueue(std::size_t max) : capacity_(max) {}\n\n    void push(T item)\n    {\n        std::unique_lock lk(mu_);\n        cvFull_.wait(lk, [&] { return queue_.size() < capacity_; });\n        queue_.push(std::move(item));\n        cvEmpty_.notify_one();\n    }\n\n    bool pop(T &out)\n    {\n        std::unique_lock lk(mu_);\n        cvEmpty_.wait(lk, [&] { return !queue_.empty() || terminated_; });\n        if (queue_.empty()) return false; // terminated\n        out = std::move(queue_.front());\n        queue_.pop();\n        cvFull_.notify_one();\n        return true;\n    }\n\n    void terminate()\n    {\n        {\n            std::lock_guard lg(mu_);\n            terminated_ = true;\n        }\n        cvEmpty_.notify_all();\n    }\n\nprivate:\n    std::size_t                capacity_;\n    std::queue<T>              queue_;       // <-- SIMPLE FIFO, NO PRIORITY!\n    std::mutex                 mu_;\n    std::condition_variable    cvFull_, cvEmpty_;\n    bool                       terminated_ {false};\n};\n```\n\n```cpp\n// File: /app/project/src/services/scanner_svc/scanner_engine.cpp\n// Lines: 246-296\n\nclass ScannerEngine\n{\npublic:\n    explicit ScannerEngine(std::size_t workerCount = std::thread::hardware_concurrency())\n        : queue_(1024), log_(), shuttingDown_(false)\n    {\n        workerCount = std::max<std::size_t>(1, workerCount);\n        log_.log(LogLevel::kInfo, \"Initializing ScannerEngine with \", workerCount, \" workers.\");\n\n        for (std::size_t i = 0; i < workerCount; ++i)\n        {\n            workers_.emplace_back([this, i] { workerLoop(i); });\n        }\n    }\n\n    // ...\n\n    void submit(const ScanCommand &cmd)\n    {\n        if (shuttingDown_.load()) throw std::runtime_error(\"Engine is shutting down\");\n        queue_.push(cmd);  // <-- ALL commands go to same queue, regardless of tenant type\n    }\n\nprivate:\n    void workerLoop(std::size_t idx)\n    {\n        try\n        {\n            while (true)\n            {\n                ScanCommand cmd;\n                if (!queue_.pop(cmd)) break; // queue terminated\n\n                notify(EngineEvent::kScanStarted, cmd, std::nullopt);\n\n                auto strategy = makeStrategy(cmd.intensity);  // Strategy selected AFTER dequeue\n\n                ScanResult res;\n                try\n                {\n                    res = strategy->execute(cmd);\n                    notify(EngineEvent::kScanFinished, cmd, res);\n                }\n                // ...\n            }\n        }\n        // ...\n    }\n\nprivate:\n    BlockingQueue<ScanCommand>                  queue_;  // <-- SINGLE SHARED QUEUE FOR ALL TENANTS\n    std::vector<std::thread>                    workers_;\n    // ...\n};\n```\n\n### 5. Event Flow Documentation\n\n```markdown\n// File: /app/project/docs/architecture/event_flows.md\n// Lines: 13-38\n\nsequenceDiagram\n    autonumber\n    actor Client as \ud83e\uddd1\u200d\ud83d\udcbb Tenant / API Consumer\n    participant API as \ud83c\udf10 Presentation & API\n    participant ORCH as \ud83d\udd04 Orchestration\n    participant BUS as \ud83d\udce8 Event-Bus\n    participant SCN as \ud83d\udee1\ufe0f ScannerSvc (Domain)\n    participant BCK as \ud83d\udcbe BackupSvc (Domain)\n    participant INF as \ud83d\udee0\ufe0f Platform Adapter\n\n    Client->>API: POST /v1/scan\\n{asset: \"web-1\", tier:\"deep\"}\n    API->>ORCH: Cmd<InitiateSecurityScan>\n    ORCH->>BUS: Publish(Cmd<InitiateSecurityScan>)\n    %% Broadcast to interested domain services\n    BUS-->>SCN: Cmd<InitiateSecurityScan>\n    SCN->>SCN: Validate + Enrich\n    SCN->>BUS: Emit(Evt<SecurityScanStarted>)\n```\n\n### 6. ADR - Event-Driven Architecture Requirements\n\n```markdown\n// File: /app/project/docs/architecture/adr/002-event-driven-architecture.md\n// Lines: 15-27\n\nKey platform requirements:\n\n* **Scalability** \u2013 Burst to > 250 K events/s while maintaining < 200 ms P95 processing latency.\n* **Extensibility** \u2013 Add a new service (e.g., `ComplianceAuditor`) with zero downtime.\n* **Fault Isolation** \u2013 Failure in `BackupNode` must **not** block `AlertBroker`.\n* **Observability** \u2013 Every state transition must emit traceable, structured audit logs.\n* **Multi-tenant Guardrails** \u2013 Tenants demand isolated QoS & configurable SLAs.\n\nThese constraints steer us toward **Event-Driven Architecture (EDA)** built around an **asynchronous, durable, high-throughput event bus**.\n```\n\n## Analysis\n\n### 1. End-to-End Request Lifecycle\n\nThe on-demand security scan request follows this path:\n\n1. **API Gateway Entry** (`routes.cpp`):\n   - Client sends `POST /v1/security/scan` with tenant ID and scan parameters\n   - Request passes through authentication middleware and rate limiter\n   - Gateway publishes `InitiateSecurityScan` command to the event bus\n   - Client receives `202 Accepted` with correlation ID\n\n2. **Orchestration Layer** (`command_handler.cpp`):\n   - Command is consumed from the event bus\n   - Passes through Chain-of-Responsibility validation pipeline (TenantQuotaValidator, CompliancePolicyValidator)\n   - Strategy is selected based on scan type/tenant subscription\n   - Command is dispatched to appropriate executor\n\n3. **Event Bus Propagation** (`event_publisher.cpp`, `event_consumer.cpp`):\n   - Events are published asynchronously to NATS JetStream/Kafka\n   - Scanner service subscribes to `security.scan.requested` topic\n   - Messages are consumed with at-least-once semantics\n\n4. **Scanner Service** (`service_impl.cpp`):\n   - Receives scan command via gRPC or event bus\n   - Resolves appropriate IScanStrategy based on tenant's subscription plan\n   - Submits scan job to ScannerEngine\n\n5. **Scanner Engine Execution** (`scanner_engine.cpp`):\n   - **ALL scan commands are pushed to a single shared `BlockingQueue<ScanCommand>`**\n   - Worker threads pop commands from queue in FIFO order\n   - Strategy is instantiated and executed for each command\n\n### 2. Architectural Interaction - How Continuous Scans Affect PAYG Tenants\n\nThe interaction between tenant types occurs at multiple levels:\n\n**Strategy Level:**\n- `ContinuousScanStrategy` runs a background loop that continuously generates scan requests at a configured cadence (e.g., every 30 seconds)\n- `PayGScanStrategy` generates scans only when explicitly triggered by API calls\n\n**Scanner Engine Level (THE KEY BOTTLENECK):**\n- Both strategies ultimately submit `ScanCommand` objects to the same `ScannerEngine`\n- The `ScannerEngine` uses a **single shared FIFO queue** with capacity of 1024\n- Worker threads process commands strictly in arrival order\n\n**Timeline Example:**\n1. Continuous scan tenant \"enterprise-corp\" has 100 assets being scanned every 30 seconds\n2. PAYG tenant \"startup-inc\" requests an on-demand deep scan\n3. The PAYG request joins the queue behind 50-100 continuous scan jobs\n4. PAYG tenant must wait for all preceding jobs to complete\n\n### 3. Root Cause - Architectural Weakness\n\n**Primary Bottleneck: Lack of Quality of Service (QoS) / Priority Queue in ScannerEngine**\n\nThe `scanner_engine.cpp` implementation reveals the core issue:\n\n```cpp\nclass ScannerEngine\n{\nprivate:\n    BlockingQueue<ScanCommand> queue_;  // Single FIFO queue - no priority differentiation\n};\n```\n\nThe `BlockingQueue` is a simple FIFO structure with no awareness of:\n- **Tenant subscription tier** (PAYG vs Continuous)\n- **Request priority** (on-demand vs background)\n- **SLA requirements** (latency-sensitive vs batch processing)\n- **Tenant isolation** (no per-tenant quotas on queue utilization)\n\n**Secondary Contributing Factors:**\n\n1. **Shared Worker Pool**: All worker threads serve the same queue, with no reservation for high-priority work\n\n2. **No Request Classification**: While the `ScanPriority` enum exists in `payg_scan_strategy.h`, it's not used in the engine's queue:\n   ```cpp\n   enum class ScanPriority : std::uint8_t\n   {\n       Normal = 0,\n       High   = 1,\n   };\n   ```\n\n3. **Strategy Selection Too Late**: The scan strategy is selected *after* dequeueing, not before enqueueing - meaning the engine has no visibility into request urgency at scheduling time\n\n4. **No Back-pressure Differentiation**: When the queue fills up (capacity=1024), all incoming requests are blocked equally regardless of tenant type or urgency\n\n### 4. Why This Causes Latency for PAYG Tenants During Peak Hours\n\n1. **Volume Disparity**: Continuous scan tenants generate steady, high-volume workloads (scanning hundreds of assets on fixed intervals)\n\n2. **Queue Saturation**: During peak hours, continuous scan jobs fill the queue, pushing wait times from milliseconds to seconds or minutes\n\n3. **FIFO Unfairness**: PAYG on-demand scans, despite being latency-sensitive, wait behind batch background jobs\n\n4. **No Isolation**: There's no mechanism to ensure PAYG tenants get a fair share of compute resources\n\n5. **ADR Violation**: The documented requirement states \"Multi-tenant Guardrails \u2013 Tenants demand isolated QoS & configurable SLAs\" - this is not implemented at the scanner engine level\n\n## Implementation (For Code Modification Tasks)\n\nN/A - This is an architectural analysis task, not a code modification task.\n\n## Summary\n\n- **Primary finding**: The root cause of PAYG tenant latency during peak hours is the **lack of priority queue or QoS mechanism in the `ScannerEngine`**. All scan requests, regardless of tenant type or urgency, are processed through a single FIFO `BlockingQueue`, causing on-demand scans to wait behind high-volume continuous scan workloads.\n\n- **Key components**:\n  - `api_gateway/routes.cpp` - Request entry point\n  - `lib/orchestration/command_handler.cpp` - Command dispatching with Chain-of-Responsibility validation\n  - `lib/domain/strategies/payg_scan_strategy.h` - PAYG strategy implementation\n  - `lib/domain/strategies/continuous_scan_strategy.h` - Continuous scan strategy (high-volume producer)\n  - `lib/infrastructure/event_bus/` - Event-driven communication layer\n  - `services/scanner_svc/scanner_engine.cpp` - **THE BOTTLENECK** - single shared FIFO queue\n\n- **Architectural pattern**: The system correctly implements:\n  - Event-Driven Architecture with NATS JetStream/Kafka\n  - Command Pattern for request encapsulation\n  - Strategy Pattern for tenant-specific scan behavior\n  - Chain-of-Responsibility for validation pipeline\n  - Observer Pattern for metrics and audit logging\n\n  However, it **fails to implement** proper QoS/priority scheduling at the worker level.\n\n- **Recommendations**:\n  1. Replace `BlockingQueue<ScanCommand>` with a **priority queue** that respects `ScanPriority` and tenant subscription tier\n  2. Implement **separate queues** for on-demand (low-latency) vs. background (batch) workloads\n  3. Reserve a portion of worker threads for high-priority work\n  4. Add **per-tenant quotas** to prevent any single tenant from monopolizing the queue\n  5. Implement **weighted fair queuing** to ensure PAYG tenants get guaranteed compute share\n  6. Consider using **separate worker pools** for different tenant tiers (as suggested by the `maxConcurrentScans` config in `PayGScanStrategy::Config`)\n",

Command Handler - Orchestration Layer\n\n```cpp\n// File: /app/project/src/lib/orchestration/command_handler.h\n// Lines: 285-336\n\ninline CommandResult CommandHandler::Dispatch(const std::shared_ptr<ICommand>& command)\n{\n    if (!command)\n        throw std::invalid_argument(\"CommandHandler::Dispatch \u2013 command is nullptr.\");\n\n    CommandContext ctx(command);\n\n    // 1) Chain-of-Responsibility: middleware pipeline\n    for (const auto& mw : middleware_pipeline_)\n    {\n        bool proceed = false;\n        try\n        {\n            proceed = mw->Handle(ctx);\n        }\n        catch (const std::exception& ex)\n        {\n            FL360_LOG_ERROR(\"Middleware [{}] threw exception: {}\", typeid(*mw).name(), ex.what());\n            return { CommandStatus::Failed, ex.what() };\n        }\n\n        if (!proceed)\n        {\n            return { CommandStatus::Failed, \"Middleware aborted execution.\" };\n        }\n    }\n\n    // 2) Locate executor\n    std::shared_ptr<IExecutorWrapper> executor;\n    {\n        std::lock_guard lock(m_);\n        const std::type_index key(typeid(*command));\n        const auto            it = executors_.find(key);\n        if (it == executors_.end())\n        {\n            return { CommandStatus::Failed,\n                     \"No executor registered for command type: \" + std::string(key.name()) };\n        }\n        executor = it->second;\n    }\n\n    // 3) Execute\n    try\n    {\n        return executor->Execute(command, ctx);\n    }\n    catch (const std::exception& ex)\n    {\n        FL360_LOG_ERROR(\"Executor for [{}] threw exception: {}\", command->name(), ex.what());\n        return { CommandStatus::Failed, ex.what() };\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 3. Scanner Engine - THE BOTTLENECK (Single FIFO Queue)\n\n```cpp\n// File: /app/project/src/services/scanner_svc/scanner_engine.cpp\n// Lines: 198-241\n\ntemplate <typename T>\nclass BlockingQueue\n{\npublic:\n    explicit BlockingQueue(std::size_t max) : capacity_(max) {}\n\n    void push(T item)\n    {\n        std::unique_lock lk(mu_);\n        cvFull_.wait(lk, [&] { return queue_.size() < capacity_; });\n        queue_.push(std::move(item));\n        cvEmpty_.notify_one();\n    }\n\n    bool pop(T &out)\n    {\n        std::unique_lock lk(mu_);\n        cvEmpty_.wait(lk, [&] { return !queue_.empty() || terminated_; });\n        if (queue_.empty()) return false; // terminated\n        out = std::move(queue_.front());\n        queue_.pop();\n        cvFull_.notify_one();\n        return true;\n    }\n\n    void terminate()\n    {\n        {\n            std::lock_guard lg(mu_);\n            terminated_ = true;\n        }\n        cvEmpty_.notify_all();\n    }\n\nprivate:\n    std::size_t                capacity_;\n    std::queue<T>              queue_;       // <-- SIMPLE FIFO, NO PRIORITY!\n    std::mutex                 mu_;\n    std::condition_variable    cvFull_, cvEmpty_;\n    bool                       terminated_ {false};\n};\n```\n\n```cpp\n// File: /app/project/src/services/scanner_svc/scanner_engine.cpp\n// Lines: 246-296\n\nclass ScannerEngine\n{\npublic:\n    explicit ScannerEngine(std::size_t workerCount = std::thread::hardware_concurrency())\n        : queue_(1024), log_(), shuttingDown_(false)\n    {\n        workerCount = std::max<std::size_t>(1, workerCount);\n        log_.log(LogLevel::kInfo, \"Initializing ScannerEngine with \", workerCount, \" workers.\");\n\n        for (std::size_t i = 0; i < workerCount; ++i)\n        {\n            workers_.emplace_back([this, i] { workerLoop(i); });\n        }\n    }\n\n    // ...\n\n    void submit(const ScanCommand &cmd)\n    {\n        if (shuttingDown_.load()) throw std::runtime_error(\"Engine is shutting down\");\n        queue_.push(cmd);  // <-- ALL commands go to same queue, regardless of tenant type\n    }\n\nprivate:\n    void workerLoop(std::size_t idx)\n    {\n        try\n        {\n            while (true)\n            {\n                ScanCommand cmd;\n                if (!queue_.pop(cmd)) break; // queue terminated\n\n                notify(EngineEvent::kScanStarted, cmd, std::nullopt);\n\n                auto strategy = makeStrategy(cmd.intensity);  // Strategy selected AFTER dequeue\n\n                ScanResult res;\n                try\n                {\n                    res = strategy->execute(cmd);\n                    notify(EngineEvent::kScanFinished, cmd, res);\n                }\n                // ...\n            }\n        }\n        // ...\n    }\n\nprivate:\n    BlockingQueue<ScanCommand>                  queue_;  // <-- SINGLE SHARED QUEUE FOR ALL TENANTS\n    std::vector<std::thread>                    workers_;\n    // ...\n};\n```\n\n### 5. # Solution: cpp_system_security_expert_064_architectural_understanding_expert_01

## Key Files Identified

- /app/project/api/v1/openapi.yaml - REST API definition for initiating scans (`POST /tenants/{tenantId}/scans`)
- /app/project/src/services/api_gateway/routes.cpp - API Gateway route handlers, publishes `InitiateSecurityScan` to event bus
- /app/project/src/services/api_gateway/server.cpp - gRPC server implementation with validation Chain-of-Responsibility
- /app/project/src/lib/orchestration/command_handler.cpp - Command dispatching with validators and strategy execution
- /app/project/src/lib/orchestration/command_handler.h - CommandHandler interface with middleware pipeline
- /app/project/src/lib/domain/commands/scan_command.h - ScanCommand domain object with event bus publishing
- /app/project/src/lib/domain/strategies/payg_scan_strategy.h - Pay-As-You-Go strategy with worker pool and FIFO queue
- /app/project/src/lib/domain/strategies/continuous_scan_strategy.h - Continuous scan strategy with background worker loop
- /app/project/src/lib/domain/strategies/isecurity_strategy.h - Strategy interface contract
- /app/project/src/lib/infrastructure/event_bus/event_publisher.h - Async event publisher with internal queue
- /app/project/src/lib/infrastructure/event_bus/event_consumer.cpp - Kafka-based event consumer with thread pool
- /app/project/src/services/scanner_svc/service_impl.cpp - Scanner gRPC service implementation
- /app/project/src/services/scanner_svc/scanner_engine.cpp - **Core scanner engine with shared FIFO work queue (bottleneck)**
- /app/project/src/services/scanner_svc/scanner_engine.h - Scanner engine interface and data structures
- /app/project/docs/architecture/event_flows.md - Event flow documentation showing request lifecycle
- /app/project/do
